/*
The program enters into an infinite loop because it continuously subtracts the divisor
from the remainder. In this case, the remainder is 10 and the divisor is 0, so remainder
will always remain as 10, which is greater than 0. This means the quotient continuously 
increments while the remainder stays the same. We would theoretically error check at the
beginning to see if the divisor is 0, and would branch to the end of the program if it was.
*/
